# MASTER CAREER REFERENCE DATABASE 2026
### AI-Powered Career Coaching Platform — Comprehensive Global Knowledge Base
**Last Updated: March 2026 | Version 4.0 — COMPLETE (48 Sections)**

> This document is the master reference database for the Shahzad Job Coach AI platform. It covers occupations, countries, salaries, skills, certifications, visas, immigration programs, recruiting firms, interview patterns, technologies, and more — globally and comprehensively.

## 3. USA SALARY TRENDS 2026

> **Sources:** U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics (bls.gov), Glassdoor (glassdoor.com), LinkedIn Salary (linkedin.com/salary), Levels.fyi (levels.fyi), Payscale (payscale.com), Compensation.cafe

### Overview
- US median household income 2026: ~$82,000
- US median individual income: ~$58,000
- Remote work premium: 5–15% above local market in lower-cost states; at-par or slight discount in HCOL markets
- Cost of living varies by up to 3x between states (San Francisco vs. Mississippi)

### Remote Work Salary Premiums / Penalties (2026)
- Fully remote roles at FAANG-level companies: typically pegged to HQ or employee location (may adjust for geo)
- Companies like Stripe, GitLab, Automattic pay location-adjusted global salaries
- Hybrid roles in NYC/SF/Seattle: premium of 10–20% vs. pure remote
- Remote-first companies in lower LCOL markets (e.g., Mid-West, South): may offer 5–10% below HCOL equivalents but purchasing power is higher

## 4. JOB DESCRIPTIONS — ALL TYPES

### Software Engineer — Full Stack
**Job Title:** Senior Full Stack Software Engineer
**Location:** Remote / Hybrid / [City, State]
**Salary Range:** $150,000 – $220,000 + equity + benefits

**About the Role:**
We are seeking an experienced Full Stack Software Engineer to design, develop, and maintain scalable web applications. You will work closely with product managers, designers, and other engineers to deliver high-quality software.

**Responsibilities:**
- Design, develop, and maintain full-stack web applications using React/Next.js (frontend) and Node.js/Python (backend)
- Build and optimize RESTful APIs and GraphQL endpoints
- Collaborate on system architecture decisions for scalability and performance
- Write clean, testable, well-documented code with unit and integration tests
- Participate in code reviews and contribute to engineering best practices
- Work in an Agile/Scrum environment with 2-week sprints
- Mentor junior engineers and contribute to team growth
- Monitor production systems using observability tools (Datadog, PagerDuty)

**Required Qualifications:**
- 5+ years of software engineering experience
- Proficiency in JavaScript/TypeScript, Python, or Go
- Experience with React, Next.js, or Vue.js
- Backend expertise: Node.js, Django, FastAPI, or Spring Boot
- Database experience: PostgreSQL, MySQL, MongoDB, Redis
- Cloud experience: AWS, GCP, or Azure
- CI/CD pipelines (GitHub Actions, Jenkins, GitLab CI)
- Containerization: Docker, Kubernetes
- Strong understanding of data structures, algorithms, and system design

**Nice to Have:**
- Experience with microservices architecture
- GraphQL expertise
- Kafka or event-driven architecture experience
- Open source contributions

**Keywords:** React, Node.js, TypeScript, PostgreSQL, AWS, Docker, Kubernetes, GraphQL, REST API, CI/CD, Agile

---

### Data Scientist
**Job Title:** Data Scientist — Machine Learning
**Salary Range:** $130,000 – $200,000 + equity

**Responsibilities:**
- Build and deploy ML models for prediction, classification, recommendation, and NLP tasks
- Conduct exploratory data analysis (EDA) and feature engineering
- Collaborate with data engineers on data pipelines and feature stores
- Deploy models to production and monitor for data drift and performance decay
- Present insights and model results to business stakeholders
- Design A/B tests and analyze results

**Required Qualifications:**
- MS/PhD in Statistics, Computer Science, Mathematics, or equivalent
- 3+ years of applied ML experience
- Expert-level Python (pandas, NumPy, scikit-learn, PyTorch or TensorFlow)
- Experience with SQL and large-scale data processing (Spark, BigQuery)
- Knowledge of statistical modeling, regression, classification, clustering
- Experience with model deployment (Docker, FastAPI, SageMaker, Vertex AI)
- Strong communication skills to translate technical findings to business

**Keywords:** Python, Machine Learning, PyTorch, TensorFlow, SQL, Spark, Scikit-learn, A/B Testing, Statistics, NLP, MLflow

---

### Product Manager
**Job Title:** Senior Product Manager
**Salary Range:** $140,000 – $210,000 + equity

**Responsibilities:**
- Own the product roadmap for a specific product area
- Define and prioritize features based on customer research, business goals, and technical feasibility
- Write detailed product requirements documents (PRDs) and user stories
- Partner with engineering, design, marketing, sales, and customer success
- Define and track product KPIs and OKRs
- Conduct user interviews, surveys, and usability studies
- Drive go-to-market strategy for new features and products
- Analyze product usage data using Amplitude, Mixpanel, or similar

**Required Qualifications:**
- 4+ years of product management experience in a tech company
- Demonstrated ability to ship products used at scale
- Strong analytical skills and comfort with data (SQL, BI tools)
- Excellent communication and stakeholder management
- Experience with Agile product development
- Background in B2B SaaS, consumer tech, or platform products preferred

**Keywords:** Product Roadmap, PRD, Agile, OKR, KPI, User Research, A/B Testing, Jira, SQL, Go-to-Market

---

### Marketing Manager
**Job Title:** Digital Marketing Manager
**Salary Range:** $80,000 – $135,000

**Responsibilities:**
- Plan and execute digital marketing campaigns across SEO, SEM, social media, email, and content
- Manage marketing budget and optimize ROI across channels
- Lead content marketing strategy including blog, webinars, case studies, and whitepapers
- Oversee SEO strategy and coordinate with content writers
- Manage paid advertising (Google Ads, LinkedIn Ads, Meta Ads)
- Analyze campaign performance and report to leadership
- Manage CRM and marketing automation (HubSpot, Marketo, Salesforce)
- Collaborate with sales for lead nurturing and pipeline generation

**Required Qualifications:**
- 4+ years digital marketing experience
- Proficiency in Google Analytics 4, HubSpot, Salesforce
- SEO/SEM expertise (Google Ads certified preferred)
- Strong copywriting and communication skills
- Experience with A/B testing and CRO (Conversion Rate Optimization)
- Marketing automation experience (Marketo, Pardot, HubSpot)
- Data-driven mindset with SQL or BI tool familiarity

**Keywords:** SEO, SEM, Google Analytics, HubSpot, Content Marketing, Email Marketing, CRM, Demand Generation, B2B Marketing

---

### Financial Analyst
**Job Title:** Financial Analyst — FP&A
**Salary Range:** $75,000 – $125,000

**Responsibilities:**
- Build and maintain financial models, forecasts, and budgets
- Analyze financial performance versus budget and prior year
- Prepare monthly management reporting packages
- Support annual budgeting and quarterly forecasting processes
- Conduct business case analysis and ROI analysis for strategic initiatives
- Partner with business unit leaders to provide financial insights
- Automate reporting using Excel, Power BI, or Tableau
- Support CFO with board reporting and investor materials

**Required Qualifications:**
- Bachelor's in Finance, Accounting, Economics, or Business
- 2–5 years financial analysis experience
- Advanced Excel (pivot tables, VLOOKUP, advanced modeling)
- Experience with ERP systems (SAP, Oracle, NetSuite, Workday)
- Power BI or Tableau preferred
- CFA Level 1 or pursuing is a plus
- Strong attention to detail and organizational skills

**Keywords:** FP&A, Financial Modeling, Excel, Forecasting, Budgeting, Power BI, SAP, Oracle, CFA, DCF, Variance Analysis

---

### Registered Nurse (RN)
**Job Title:** Registered Nurse — Medical/Surgical Unit
**Salary Range:** $68,000 – $105,000 (+ differentials for nights, weekends, holidays)

**Responsibilities:**
- Provide direct patient care in accordance with care plans and physician orders
- Assess patient conditions, administer medications, and document in EHR (Epic, Cerner)
- Communicate with physicians, specialists, and interdisciplinary teams
- Educate patients and families on diagnoses, medications, and discharge instructions
- Monitor vital signs, lab results, and patient status changes
- Respond to patient emergencies and initiate emergency protocols
- Mentor nursing students and new staff
- Maintain compliance with Joint Commission standards

**Required Qualifications:**
- Active RN license (state-specific; compact license preferred)
- BSN preferred; ADN with BSN program enrollment acceptable
- BLS, ACLS certifications required
- 1+ years acute care nursing experience
- Epic or Cerner EHR experience preferred
- Strong clinical assessment and critical thinking skills

**Keywords:** RN, BSN, ACLS, BLS, Epic, Cerner, Patient Care, Medical-Surgical, ICU, ER Nursing

### Physician (MD) — General Practice / Family Medicine
**Job Title:** Family Medicine Physician
**Salary Range:** $220,000 – $310,000

**Responsibilities:**
- Provide comprehensive primary care to patients of all ages
- Diagnose and treat acute and chronic conditions
- Manage preventive care, wellness exams, and immunizations
- Order and interpret diagnostic tests (labs, imaging)
- Prescribe medications and manage chronic disease panels (diabetes, hypertension, etc.)
- Refer patients to specialists as appropriate
- Document encounters in EHR (Epic, Cerner, Athena)
- Participate in quality improvement and value-based care initiatives

**Required Qualifications:**
- MD or DO from accredited medical school
- Board-certified or board-eligible in Family Medicine
- Active state medical license and DEA number
- Completion of accredited residency program
- Current BLS/ACLS certification
- Malpractice insurance

**Keywords:** MD, DO, Board Certified, Family Medicine, Primary Care, Epic, EHR, DEA, ABFM, Patient-Centered Care

- Commitment to equity and culturally responsive teaching

### Cybersecurity Analyst
**Job Title:** Senior Cybersecurity Analyst — SOC
**Salary Range:** $100,000 – $160,000

**Responsibilities:**
- Monitor SIEM platforms (Splunk, IBM QRadar, Microsoft Sentinel) for security events
- Investigate and triage security alerts (Tier 2/3 level)
- Conduct threat hunting using MITRE ATT&CK framework
- Respond to security incidents and lead incident response process
- Perform vulnerability assessments and coordinate remediation
- Write and review detection rules, playbooks, and runbooks
- Conduct phishing simulations and security awareness training
- Collaborate with IT and DevSecOps on security controls
- Prepare security reports for management

**Required Qualifications:**
- 4+ years cybersecurity experience
- CISSP, CISM, CEH, or CompTIA Security+ certification
- SIEM experience (Splunk preferred)
- Knowledge of MITRE ATT&CK, Kill Chain, NIST CSF
- Incident response and forensics experience
- Network security: firewalls, IDS/IPS, VPN, NAC
- Cloud security experience (AWS Security Hub, Azure Defender)

**Keywords:** SOC, SIEM, Splunk, MITRE ATT&CK, Incident Response, CISSP, Threat Hunting, Vulnerability Management, NIST CSF

### Social Worker
**Job Title:** Licensed Clinical Social Worker (LCSW)
**Salary Range:** $58,000 – $95,000

**Responsibilities:**
- Provide individual, group, and family therapy services
- Conduct psychosocial assessments and develop treatment plans
- Manage a caseload of clients with mental health, substance abuse, or social needs
- Coordinate with multidisciplinary teams (psychiatrists, nurses, case managers)
- Maintain client records and documentation in EHR systems
- Advocate for clients' rights and access to community resources
- Provide crisis intervention and safety planning
- Supervise MSW-level social work interns
- Maintain compliance with HIPAA and professional ethical standards

**Required Qualifications:**
- Master of Social Work (MSW) from CSWE-accredited program
- LCSW license (state-specific)
- 2+ years post-licensure clinical experience
- Experience with CBT, DBT, trauma-informed care, or motivational interviewing
- Electronic health record experience
- Strong empathy, active listening, and boundary-setting skills

**Keywords:** LCSW, MSW, Clinical Social Work, CBT, DBT, Trauma-Informed Care, Mental Health, Case Management, HIPAA, Therapy

### Additional Job Description Templates (Summary Format)

**Cloud Architect:** Design AWS/Azure/GCP multi-region architectures; require 7+ yrs cloud exp, AWS SA Professional or Azure Solutions Architect Expert cert; $160K–$250K.

**Data Engineer:** Build and maintain data pipelines (Airflow, Spark, dbt, Kafka); require Python, SQL, cloud data warehouse experience (Snowflake, BigQuery, Redshift); $120K–$190K.

**Mechanical Engineer — Product Development:** CAD design (SolidWorks, CATIA), FEA simulation, GD&T, DFM/DFA, product lifecycle management; $80K–$140K.

**Biomedical Engineer:** Medical device design, FDA 510(k) submissions, ISO 13485, design controls, usability engineering; $80K–$140K.

**Environmental Engineer:** NEPA compliance, remediation design, stormwater management, air quality permitting, EPA regulations; $68K–$120K.

**Network Engineer:** Cisco/Juniper routing/switching, BGP/OSPF, SD-WAN, firewall management, VPN; CCNA/CCNP required; $85K–$145K.

**Healthcare Administrator:** Hospital operations, budget management, Joint Commission compliance, patient satisfaction, Epic administration; $85K–$165K.

**Pharmacist (Clinical):** MTM (Medication Therapy Management), oncology/critical care/ambulatory care specialties; PharmD + licensure; $125K–$160K.

**Public Health Analyst:** Epidemiological surveillance, health equity analysis, CDC/state health department reporting, SAS/R/Python; $65K–$105K.

**Grant Writer:** Non-profit fundraising, federal (NIH, NSF, SAMHSA) and private grants, Logic Models, program evaluation; $55K–$90K.

**Technical Recruiter:** Full-cycle tech recruiting, Boolean searches, ATS (Greenhouse, Lever, Workday), sourcing on LinkedIn; $70K–$130K + commission.

**Logistics Coordinator:** Freight tracking, carrier negotiations, customs documentation, TMS systems, international trade; $50K–$80K.

**Real Estate Agent:** Buyer/seller representation, MLS, CMA analysis, contract negotiations; commission-based ($50K–$300K+).

**Executive Assistant (C-Suite):** Calendar management, travel coordination, board meeting prep, confidential correspondence; $80K–$130K.

**Investment Banking Analyst:** Financial modeling, pitch books, LBO analysis, DCF, comps; $110K–$150K base + $50K–$80K bonus.

**Clinical Research Coordinator:** IRB submissions, protocol adherence, patient consent, data management (EDC), GCP compliance; $55K–$85K.

**Occupational Therapist:** ADL assessment, sensory integration, adaptive equipment, SOAP notes, school or hospital setting; $75K–$105K.

**Speech-Language Pathologist:** Dysphagia, articulation, language disorders, AAC devices, pediatric or adult settings; $78K–$110K.

**Dental Hygienist:** Prophylaxis, periodontal charting, patient education, digital radiography, infection control; $68K–$95K.

**Physical Therapist (PT):** Orthopedic or neuro rehab, manual therapy, therapeutic exercise, functional mobility; $80K–$105K.

**Radiologic Technologist:** CT, MRI, X-ray imaging, ARRT certification, HIPAA compliance; $60K–$90K.

**Embedded Systems Engineer:** C/C++, RTOS, microcontrollers (ARM, STM32), device drivers, hardware-software co-design; $95K–$165K.

**Aerospace Systems Engineer:** Systems engineering lifecycle, requirements management, MBSE (SysML), DO-178C, MIL-STD; $100K–$180K.

**Petroleum Engineer:** Reservoir simulation (Eclipse, CMG), well design, production optimization, petrophysical analysis; $95K–$180K.

**Food Scientist:** Product formulation, FSMA, HACCP, shelf-life testing, sensory evaluation, FDA/USDA regulations; $65K–$105K.

**ESG Analyst:** GRI/SASB/TCFD reporting, carbon accounting, stakeholder engagement, ESG data platforms; $80K–$140K.

**Instructional Designer:** ADDIE/SAM models, Articulate Storyline, LMS (Moodle, Cornerstone), needs analysis; $65K–$105K.

**AI Ethicist:** Responsible AI frameworks, bias auditing, model transparency, policy development, stakeholder education; $110K–$180K.

**Prompt Engineer:** LLM optimization, prompt chaining, RAG architecture, system prompt design, evaluation frameworks; $90K–$180K.

## 5. HARD SKILLS — A TO Z ALL INDUSTRIES

### Programming Languages
- Python — most versatile; AI/ML, web, automation, data science
- JavaScript — web frontend and backend (Node.js); most used language globally
- TypeScript — JavaScript with static types; dominant in enterprise frontend
- Java — enterprise backend, Android, Spring Boot ecosystem
- C — systems programming, embedded, OS kernels
- C++ — performance-critical software, game engines, HFT, simulation
- C# — Microsoft ecosystem, Unity game development, .NET
- Go (Golang) — cloud-native backends, Kubernetes tooling, CLI tools
- Rust — memory-safe systems programming; WebAssembly, embedded, crypto
- Ruby — web development (Rails), scripting, DevOps tooling
- PHP — web backend (WordPress, Laravel, Symfony); powers 75%+ of CMS
- Swift — iOS/macOS app development; Apple ecosystem
- Kotlin — Android development; JVM alternative to Java
- Dart — Flutter cross-platform apps (Google)
- R — statistical computing, bioinformatics, data visualization
- MATLAB — engineering simulation, signal processing, control systems
- Scala — big data (Apache Spark), functional programming, JVM
- Perl — legacy system administration, text processing, bioinformatics
- Lua — embedded scripting (game engines, Nginx, embedded devices)
- Haskell — functional programming, academic research, financial modeling
- Elixir — fault-tolerant distributed systems (Erlang VM, Phoenix framework)
- Clojure — JVM Lisp; data transformation, functional programming
- Julia — scientific computing, numerical analysis, HPC
- Groovy — JVM scripting; Gradle build scripts, Jenkins pipelines
- COBOL — legacy banking, government, insurance mainframe systems
- Fortran — scientific and numerical computing; HPC legacy
- Assembly Language — low-level hardware programming, reverse engineering
- Bash / Shell Scripting — Linux automation, CI/CD scripts, DevOps
- PowerShell — Windows automation, Azure administration
- SQL — relational database querying; essential across all data roles
- PL/SQL — Oracle stored procedures and functions
- T-SQL — Microsoft SQL Server stored procedures
- HiveQL — querying Hadoop-based data warehouses
- GraphQL — API query language; alternative to REST
- HTML5 — web markup; structure of web pages
- CSS3 / Sass / LESS — web styling and layout
- Solidity — Ethereum smart contracts
- Vyper — Python-like Ethereum smart contract language
- VHDL / Verilog — hardware description languages for FPGAs and ASICs
- LabVIEW — National Instruments platform for instrumentation and test
- Prolog — logic programming; AI research
- Erlang — distributed systems, telecom, real-time applications

### Frontend Development
- React.js — component-based UI library; most popular frontend framework
- Next.js — React framework with SSR, SSG, App Router; Vercel ecosystem
- Vue.js — progressive JavaScript framework; popular in Asia-Pacific
- Angular — TypeScript-based SPA framework; Google; enterprise apps
- Svelte — compiler-based UI framework; no virtual DOM; rising rapidly
- Astro — content-first web framework; islands architecture
- Tailwind CSS — utility-first CSS framework; dominant in modern web dev
- Bootstrap — responsive CSS framework; legacy and rapid prototyping
- Material UI (MUI) — Google Material Design for React
- Shadcn/ui — component library built on Radix UI and Tailwind
- Webpack / Vite / Parcel / Rollup — module bundlers and build tools
- Jest / Vitest — unit testing for JavaScript/TypeScript
- Cypress / Playwright — end-to-end browser testing
- Storybook — component documentation and visual testing
- Three.js — 3D graphics in the browser (WebGL)
- D3.js — data-driven document manipulation and visualization

### Backend Development
- Node.js / Express.js / Fastify / NestJS — JavaScript server-side
- Django / Flask / FastAPI — Python web frameworks
- Spring Boot / Spring Framework — Java enterprise backend
- Ruby on Rails — convention-over-configuration MVC framework
- Laravel / Symfony — PHP frameworks
- ASP.NET Core — Microsoft C# framework; Azure-native
- Gin / Fiber / Echo — Go web frameworks
- Actix-Web / Axum — Rust web frameworks
- gRPC — high-performance RPC; Protocol Buffers; inter-service communication
- REST API Design — stateless, resource-based HTTP API design
- WebSockets — full-duplex real-time communication
- GraphQL Server — flexible API queries (Apollo Server, Hasura)
- Apache Kafka — distributed event streaming platform
- RabbitMQ — message broker; AMQP protocol
- Redis — in-memory data structure store; caching, queues, pub/sub
- OAuth 2.0 / OpenID Connect — authorization and authentication standards
- JWT (JSON Web Tokens) — stateless authentication tokens
- SAML — enterprise SSO federation
- OpenAPI / Swagger — API documentation and design specification

### Cloud — AWS Services
- EC2, S3, RDS, Aurora, DynamoDB, Lambda, ECS, EKS, ECR, CloudFront
- Route 53, VPC, IAM, CloudWatch, CloudTrail, SNS, SQS, Kinesis
- Glue, Athena, Redshift, SageMaker, Bedrock, OpenSearch
- CloudFormation, CDK, Fargate, Step Functions
- Secrets Manager, WAF, Shield, GuardDuty, Security Hub

### Cloud — Azure Services
- Azure VMs, Blob Storage, SQL Database, Cosmos DB, Functions, AKS
- App Service, Entra ID (Azure AD), Azure DevOps, Monitor, Log Analytics
- Event Hub, Service Bus, Data Factory, Synapse Analytics
- Azure Machine Learning, Azure OpenAI Service, Cognitive Services
- Bicep / ARM Templates, Key Vault, Front Door, API Management
- Microsoft Defender for Cloud, Microsoft Sentinel (SIEM)

### Cloud — GCP Services
- Compute Engine, Cloud Storage, Cloud SQL, BigQuery, Cloud Run, GKE
- Cloud Functions, Pub/Sub, Dataflow, Vertex AI, Looker Studio
- Cloud Armor, Spanner, Firebase, Apigee, Artifact Registry

### Databases
- PostgreSQL — most advanced open-source relational DB; JSON support
- MySQL / MariaDB — widely used RDBMS; LAMP stack
- Microsoft SQL Server / Oracle Database — enterprise RDBMS
- MongoDB — document-oriented NoSQL; JSON/BSON documents
- Cassandra — wide-column NoSQL; high write throughput; time-series
- DynamoDB — AWS fully managed NoSQL; serverless scaling
- Redis — key-value store; caching, sessions, leaderboards
- Elasticsearch / OpenSearch — full-text search and analytics
- Neo4j — graph database; knowledge graphs, fraud detection
- InfluxDB / TimescaleDB — time-series databases; IoT, metrics
- ClickHouse — columnar OLAP database; real-time analytics
- Snowflake — cloud data warehouse; multi-cloud; data sharing
- Databricks (Delta Lake) — unified analytics platform; lakehouse architecture
- Amazon Redshift — AWS cloud data warehouse
- Supabase — open-source Firebase alternative; PostgreSQL-based
- CockroachDB / YugabyteDB — distributed SQL; cloud-native

### DevOps & Infrastructure Tools
- Docker — containerization; images, containers, Docker Compose
- Kubernetes (K8s) — container orchestration; pods, deployments, services
- Helm — Kubernetes package manager; charts
- ArgoCD / FluxCD — GitOps continuous delivery for Kubernetes
- Terraform — Infrastructure as Code (IaC); multi-cloud; HashiCorp
- Pulumi — IaC with general-purpose languages
- Ansible — agentless configuration management; YAML playbooks
- Chef / Puppet — configuration management; large-scale infrastructure
- Jenkins — open-source CI/CD automation server
- GitHub Actions — native CI/CD in GitHub repositories
- GitLab CI/CD — integrated DevOps platform
- CircleCI / Travis CI — hosted CI/CD services
- Prometheus / Grafana — metrics collection and visualization
- Datadog / New Relic / Dynatrace — APM and infrastructure monitoring
- PagerDuty / OpsGenie — on-call alerting and incident management
- Splunk / ELK Stack (Elasticsearch, Logstash, Kibana) — log management
- OpenTelemetry — vendor-neutral observability instrumentation
- Istio / Linkerd — Kubernetes service mesh
- HashiCorp Vault — secrets management
- Nginx / HAProxy / Traefik / Envoy — reverse proxies and load balancers

### AI / ML Tools & Frameworks
- TensorFlow — Google's open-source ML framework; production ML
- PyTorch — Facebook's ML framework; dominant in research and LLMs
- Keras — high-level neural network API; runs on TensorFlow/JAX
- Scikit-learn — classical ML algorithms; Python; essential for data scientists
- XGBoost / LightGBM / CatBoost — gradient boosting; tabular data
- Hugging Face Transformers — pretrained NLP models; model hub
- LangChain — framework for LLM application development
- LlamaIndex — data framework for LLM applications; RAG
- OpenAI API — GPT-4o, o3, DALL-E, Whisper, Embeddings
- Anthropic API — Claude models; constitutional AI
- Google Gemini API — multimodal LLM; Google AI Studio / Vertex AI
- Ollama — run local LLMs (LLaMA, Mistral, Gemma)
- MLflow — ML experiment tracking, model registry, deployment
- Weights & Biases (W&B) — experiment tracking and visualization
- DVC — data and model version control
- ONNX — open format for ML model interoperability
- TensorRT — NVIDIA inference optimization
- Ray — distributed computing framework for Python
- Vector Databases: Pinecone, Weaviate, Chroma, Qdrant, Milvus
- Stable Diffusion / DALL-E / Midjourney — generative image AI
- Whisper — OpenAI speech-to-text; multilingual
- RAG (Retrieval-Augmented Generation) — architecture pattern
- Fine-tuning techniques: LoRA, QLoRA, PEFT, DPO, RLHF

### Cybersecurity Tools
- Metasploit Framework — penetration testing; exploit development
- Burp Suite Pro — web application security testing; OWASP
- Nessus / Qualys / Rapid7 InsightVM — vulnerability scanning
- Nmap — network discovery and security auditing
- Wireshark — network protocol analysis
- CrowdStrike Falcon / SentinelOne — next-gen EDR/XDR
- Palo Alto Cortex XDR / Microsoft Defender XDR — extended detection
- Splunk Enterprise Security — SIEM; threat detection and response
- IBM QRadar / Microsoft Sentinel / Sumo Logic — SIEM platforms
- MITRE ATT&CK — adversary tactics and techniques knowledge base
- Ghidra / IDA Pro — reverse engineering and malware analysis
- Volatility — memory forensics
- Autopsy / FTK / EnCase — digital forensics
- Snort / Suricata — open-source IDS/IPS
- MISP / OpenCTI — threat intelligence platforms
- Okta / CyberArk / SailPoint — identity and access management (IAM)
- Tenable.io — vulnerability management cloud platform
- OWASP ZAP — open-source web app security scanner
- HashiCorp Vault — secrets and certificate management
- Falco — runtime security for containers and Kubernetes
- Veracode / Checkmarx / SonarQube — SAST code security scanning

### Data Analytics & BI
- Tableau — visual analytics platform; drag-and-drop; widely used in business
- Power BI — Microsoft's BI tool; deeply integrated with Azure and M365
- Looker / Looker Studio — Google's BI and data exploration platform
- Metabase — open-source BI; SQL and no-code queries
- Apache Superset — open-source data exploration and visualization
- dbt (Data Build Tool) — SQL-based data transformation; analytics engineering
- Apache Airflow — workflow orchestration; DAG-based scheduling
- Apache Spark / PySpark — large-scale data processing; distributed computing
- Apache Kafka — real-time event streaming and data pipelines
- Fivetran / Stitch — managed ELT connectors to data warehouses
- Excel — universal business tool; advanced: Power Query, Power Pivot, VBA
- SPSS / SAS — statistical analysis; legacy enterprise use; healthcare research
- Databricks — unified data + AI platform; Apache Spark + Delta Lake

### ERP, CRM & Enterprise Platforms
- SAP S/4HANA — SAP's flagship ERP; Finance (FICO), Logistics (MM, SD), HR (HCM), Manufacturing (PP)
- SAP Ariba — procurement and supply chain management
- Oracle ERP Cloud / Oracle Fusion — cloud-native ERP
- Microsoft Dynamics 365 — Business Central (SMB) and F&O (enterprise)
- Salesforce CRM — Sales Cloud, Service Cloud, Marketing Cloud, Commerce Cloud
- HubSpot — inbound marketing and CRM for SMBs
- ServiceNow — ITSM, HRSD, CSM, GRC, SecOps
- Workday — cloud HCM and Financial Management
- NetSuite — Oracle's cloud ERP for mid-market
- Greenhouse / Lever / iCIMS / Taleo — Applicant Tracking Systems (ATS)
- ADP / Paychex — payroll and HR administration
- BambooHR / Rippling / Gusto — SMB HR platforms

### Finance Tools
- Bloomberg Terminal — real-time financial data, analytics, news; $25K+/yr
- FactSet / Capital IQ / PitchBook — financial research and data
- Morningstar Direct — investment research and portfolio analytics
- QuickBooks / Xero / Sage Intacct — small business accounting
- Excel Financial Modeling — DCF, LBO, M&A, three-statement models
- Argus Enterprise — commercial real estate valuation and analysis
- Advent Portfolio Exchange (APX) — portfolio management (investment firms)
- SS&C Eze / Charles River — order management systems (OMS) for asset managers
- Roper / FIS / Broadridge — capital markets technology

### Healthcare IT Tools
- Epic EHR — largest US hospital EHR; MyChart patient portal
- Oracle Health (Cerner) — major EHR competitor to Epic
- Meditech Expanse — community hospital EHR
- Athenahealth — ambulatory EHR and RCM platform
- PACS/RIS — radiology picture archiving and information systems
- HL7 FHIR — API-based healthcare data interoperability
- Allscripts / eClinicalWorks — ambulatory care EHR
- Pyxis / Omnicell — automated pharmacy dispensing systems

### Industrial / OT Technologies
- SCADA Systems (Wonderware/AVEVA, Ignition, Siemens WinCC)
- PLC Programming (Allen-Bradley/Rockwell, Siemens S7, Mitsubishi)
- DCS (Honeywell Experion, ABB 800xA, Emerson DeltaV)
- Modbus / EtherCAT / PROFIBUS / OPC-UA — industrial communication protocols
- Historian Systems (OSIsoft PI, Aspentech IP.21) — industrial data
- CMMS (Maximo, SAP PM, eMaint) — computerized maintenance management
- Digital Twin Platforms (Siemens, ANSYS, PTC ThingWorx)

### Collaboration & Productivity Tools
- Slack — team messaging; most popular in tech companies
- Microsoft Teams — enterprise collaboration; M365 integrated
- Zoom — video conferencing; meeting-first platform
- Google Workspace — Gmail, Drive, Docs, Sheets, Meet; dominant in startups
- Jira — project tracking; Agile boards; Atlassian
- Confluence — team knowledge base and documentation; Atlassian
- Notion — all-in-one workspace; notes, databases, wikis, projects
- Asana / Monday.com / ClickUp — project and work management
- Linear — modern issue tracker; popular with engineering teams
- Trello — Kanban boards; Atlassian; visual task management
- Miro — online collaborative whiteboard
- Loom — async video messaging for remote teams
- Figma — collaborative design; browser-based; real-time multiplayer
- Coda — document + spreadsheet + app builder hybrid

### Mobile Development
- React Native — cross-platform mobile apps with React
- Flutter — Google's Dart-based cross-platform framework
- SwiftUI — declarative UI for Apple platforms (iOS, macOS, watchOS, tvOS)
- Jetpack Compose — modern Android UI toolkit; Kotlin
- Ionic — web-based cross-platform mobile apps
- Capacitor — bridge for web apps to run as native mobile apps

### Blockchain & Web3
- Ethereum / Solidity — most popular smart contract platform
- Web3.js / Ethers.js — JavaScript libraries for Ethereum interaction
- Hardhat / Foundry / Truffle — development environments for smart contracts
- OpenZeppelin — secure smart contract libraries
- IPFS — InterPlanetary File System; decentralized storage
- Polygon / Arbitrum / Optimism / zkSync — Layer 2 scaling solutions
- Solana — high-speed blockchain; Rust + Anchor framework
- Hyperledger Fabric — enterprise permissioned blockchain (Linux Foundation)
- Chainlink — decentralized oracle network
- MetaMask / WalletConnect — wallet standards

### Telecommunications
- 5G NR (New Radio) — sub-6 GHz and mmWave; network slicing; URLLC, eMBB
- LTE / 4G — still dominant globally; LTE-A, VoLTE
- Wi-Fi 6 / 6E (802.11ax) — high-efficiency wireless; WPA3 security
- VoIP / SIP / WebRTC — IP-based voice and video communications
- SD-WAN — software-defined wide area networks; Cisco, VMware, Palo Alto
- NFV (Network Functions Virtualization) — software-defined network functions
- OpenRAN — disaggregated radio access networks; O-RAN Alliance
- Cisco IOS / IOS-XE / IOS-XR — Cisco router and switch operating systems
- Juniper JunOS — Juniper Networks operating system
- Network Automation (Ansible, Python Netmiko, NAPALM) — programmable networks
- NETCONF / YANG / RESTCONF — network configuration protocols

### Gaming & Creative Tech
- Unity — cross-platform game engine; mobile, PC, XR
- Unreal Engine 5 — high-fidelity AAA game engine; Lumen, Nanite
- Godot — open-source game engine; growing indie community
- Blender — open-source 3D modeling, animation, VFX, rendering
- Maya (Autodesk) — industry standard for 3D animation; film, TV, games
- Substance Painter / Substance Designer — 3D texture painting (Adobe)
- ZBrush — digital sculpting for organic models
- Adobe Premiere Pro / DaVinci Resolve — professional video editing
- Adobe After Effects — motion graphics and VFX compositing
- Adobe Photoshop / Illustrator / InDesign — industry standard creative suite
- Figma — product and UI design; prototyping; design systems

---

## 6. SOFT SKILLS — COMPLETE LIST

### Communication
- **Verbal Communication** — Articulating ideas clearly in spoken form; critical in presentations, meetings, client-facing roles
- **Written Communication** — Clear, concise, persuasive writing; essential for emails, reports, proposals, documentation
- **Active Listening** — Fully concentrating, understanding, and responding; builds trust and reduces misunderstandings
- **Presentation Skills** — Engaging audiences in formal settings; required for leadership, sales, and technical roles
- **Storytelling** — Using narrative to make data and ideas compelling; powerful in leadership and marketing
- **Cross-Cultural Communication** — Adapting communication styles across cultures; essential in global teams
- **Technical Communication** — Translating complex concepts for non-technical audiences
- **Feedback Delivery** — Giving constructive, actionable feedback; required for managers and team leads
- **Nonverbal Communication** — Body language, eye contact, tone; shapes impressions in interviews and negotiations
- **Digital Communication Etiquette** — Professionalism in email, Slack, Zoom, and async tools
- **Public Speaking** — Confidence before large audiences; Toastmasters, TEDx-style delivery
- **Persuasive Writing** — Grant proposals, executive memos, sales copy; moves people to action
- **Negotiation Communication** — Language frameworks for reaching mutually beneficial agreements

### Leadership & Management
- **Strategic Thinking** — Connecting day-to-day work to long-term goals
- **Decision-Making** — Making timely, well-reasoned decisions under uncertainty
- **People Management** — Developing, motivating, and retaining team members
- **Delegation** — Assigning tasks appropriately to maximize team productivity
- **Coaching and Mentoring** — Developing others through guidance, not just direction
- **Change Management** — Leading teams through organizational transformation
- **Conflict Resolution** — Mediating disputes and finding mutually acceptable solutions
- **Accountability** — Owning outcomes and creating a culture of responsibility
- **Executive Presence** — Projecting confidence and credibility to senior stakeholders
- **Vision Setting** — Inspiring teams with a compelling picture of the future
- **Political Savvy** — Navigating organizational dynamics constructively
- **Influence Without Authority** — Driving results without formal power; critical for ICs and PMs
- **Situational Leadership** — Adapting leadership style to team maturity and situation (Hersey & Blanchard)
- **Crisis Leadership** — Staying calm and decisive during emergencies or crises

### Emotional Intelligence (EQ)
- **Self-Awareness** — Recognizing one's emotions and their impact on behavior and decisions
- **Self-Regulation** — Managing disruptive emotions; staying composed under pressure
- **Empathy** — Understanding and sharing the feelings of others; foundational to leadership and service
- **Social Skills** — Managing relationships and building networks effectively
- **Motivation** — Inner drive to achieve beyond external rewards; linked to resilience and work ethic
- **Emotional Resilience** — Recovering quickly from setbacks and adversity
- **Vulnerability** — Willingness to acknowledge mistakes; builds psychological safety in teams
- **Patience** — Tolerating delays and frustration without losing effectiveness
- **Compassion** — Caring genuinely about the well-being of colleagues and customers

### Critical Thinking & Problem Solving
- **Analytical Thinking** — Breaking down complex problems systematically
- **Problem-Solving** — Identifying root causes and developing effective solutions
- **Creative Thinking / Innovation** — Generating novel ideas and approaches
- **Data-Driven Decision-Making** — Using evidence over intuition
- **Systems Thinking** — Understanding how parts of a system interact; needed in engineering, operations, policy
- **First-Principles Thinking** — Challenging assumptions and reasoning from foundational truths (Elon Musk, Aristotle)
- **Risk Assessment** — Identifying, evaluating, and mitigating risks before acting
- **Judgment** — Making sound decisions in ambiguous or high-stakes situations
- **Debugging Mindset** — Systematically isolating variables to find root cause (software and beyond)
- **Research Skills** — Finding, evaluating, and synthesizing information effectively
- **Hypothesis-Driven Thinking** — Forming testable hypotheses; scientific method applied to business

### Teamwork & Collaboration
- **Collaboration** — Working effectively with diverse teams toward common goals
- **Cross-Functional Collaboration** — Partnering with people from different departments and disciplines
- **Psychological Safety** — Creating environments where team members feel safe speaking up (Amy Edmondson, Google Project Aristotle)
- **Inclusivity** — Actively welcoming diverse perspectives and contributions
- **Team Building** — Forming and developing cohesive, high-performing teams
- **Knowledge Sharing** — Freely sharing expertise to elevate the team
- **Constructive Disagreement** — Challenging ideas respectfully to improve outcomes
- **Remote Collaboration** — Working effectively with distributed teams across time zones and cultures
- **Meeting Facilitation** — Running productive, outcome-focused meetings

### Adaptability & Learning
- **Adaptability** — Adjusting to changing conditions, priorities, and environments
- **Learning Agility** — Ability to learn quickly from experience and apply it to new situations
- **Growth Mindset** — Believing abilities can be developed through dedication (Carol Dweck's research)
- **Intellectual Curiosity** — Intrinsic motivation to explore, question, and understand
- **Resilience** — Maintaining effectiveness in the face of obstacles, setbacks, or failure
- **Ambiguity Tolerance** — Functioning effectively when goals, processes, or information are unclear
- **Continuous Learning** — Commitment to professional development; staying current in one's field
- **Unlearning** — Letting go of outdated assumptions and methods to adopt new, better ones

### Time Management & Productivity
- **Time Management** — Planning and prioritizing work to meet deadlines
- **Prioritization** — Distinguishing urgent from important; aligning effort to highest value
- **Organization** — Maintaining structured systems for tasks, information, and communication
- **Goal Setting** — Defining specific, measurable, achievable objectives (OKRs, SMART goals)
- **Focus / Deep Work** — Sustained concentration on demanding cognitive tasks (Cal Newport's Deep Work)
- **Deadline Management** — Consistently delivering on commitments
- **Energy Management** — Managing personal energy levels for sustained high performance
- **Autonomy** — Working effectively with minimal supervision; key in remote and senior roles
- **Saying No Effectively** — Protecting focus by declining low-value work diplomatically

### Interpersonal Skills
- **Networking** — Building and maintaining mutually beneficial professional relationships
- **Persuasion** — Convincing others through evidence, logic, and emotional appeal (Cialdini's influence principles)
- **Negotiation** — Reaching agreements that serve all parties' core interests (Fisher & Ury: Getting to Yes)
- **Relationship Building** — Developing trust and rapport over time with colleagues, clients, and stakeholders
- **Customer Service Orientation** — Centering the customer experience in every interaction
- **Diplomacy** — Handling sensitive situations with tact and discretion
- **Cultural Competence** — Effectively working with people from diverse cultural backgrounds
- **Humility** — Acknowledging one's limitations and giving credit to others
- **Reliability** — Consistently following through on commitments; being trusted to deliver

### Professional Attributes
- **Work Ethic** — Commitment to giving full effort in all tasks
- **Integrity** — Acting with honesty and strong moral principles
- **Professionalism** — Maintaining appropriate conduct in all work contexts
- **Initiative** — Taking action without being asked; proactively identifying and solving problems
- **Ownership / Accountability** — Taking full responsibility for outcomes
- **Grit** — Long-term passion and perseverance (Angela Duckworth's research)
- **Detail Orientation** — Noticing and correcting small errors; critical in finance, law, engineering, medicine
- **Big-Picture Thinking** — Seeing beyond immediate tasks to broader context and implications
- **Confidentiality** — Handling sensitive information with discretion
- **Ethical Judgment** — Making decisions aligned with professional ethics and organizational values
- **Self-Motivation** — Sustaining effort and direction without external prodding
- **Coachability** — Openness to feedback and willingness to change behavior

### Specialized Soft Skills (Industry-Specific)
- **Bedside Manner** (Healthcare) — Building trust and comfort with patients during vulnerable moments
- **Classroom Management** (Education) — Maintaining an effective, inclusive learning environment
- **Courtroom Presence** (Legal) — Commanding attention and credibility in legal proceedings
- **Donor Relations** (Non-Profit) — Cultivating relationships with philanthropic supporters
- **Stakeholder Management** (PM/Consulting) — Balancing diverse stakeholder interests and expectations
- **C-Suite Communication** (Business) — Presenting confidently to board and executive leadership
- **Sales Intuition** (Sales) — Reading customer needs, timing, and buying signals
- **Design Thinking** (Product/UX) — Empathy-driven, iterative human-centered problem-solving
- **Regulatory Mindset** (Finance/Healthcare/Legal) — Natural instinct to consider compliance implications
- **Trauma-Informed Practice** (Social Work/Mental Health) — Understanding impact of trauma on behavior
- **Curatorial Eye** (Arts/Media) — Aesthetic judgment and taste in selecting and presenting creative work
- **Athletic Coaching** (Sports) — Motivating and developing physical performance in athletes

---

## 7. RESUME AND CV TEMPLATES BY COUNTRY

### United States (USA)
**Format:** Resume (not CV unless for academic/research positions)
**Length:** 1 page (0–5 yrs experience); 2 pages (5–15 yrs); 3+ pages only for executive or academic
**File Format:** PDF preferred for human review; both PDF and DOCX may be required for ATS
**Font:** Calibri, Arial, Helvetica, Garamond; 10–12pt body; consistent formatting
**Margins:** 0.5–1 inch; avoid tiny margins

**Section Order:**
1. Name + Contact (phone, professional email, LinkedIn URL, GitHub/portfolio link)
2. Professional Summary (3–4 lines; tailored per application — not a generic objective)
3. Work Experience (reverse chronological; bullet points with action verbs + quantified metrics)
4. Education (degree, institution, graduation year; GPA optional if 3.5+; include honors)
5. Technical Skills (tools, technologies, certifications)
6. Optional: Projects, Publications, Volunteer Work, Awards, Professional Memberships

**Writing Style:** Achievement-focused bullet points: "Led migration of monolithic app to microservices, reducing latency by 40% and deployment time from 2 days to 4 hours"
**ATS Optimization:** Include exact keywords from job description; avoid tables, columns, text boxes, headers/footers, embedded images (ATS cannot parse them)
**What to EXCLUDE:** Photo, age, date of birth, marital status, national ID number, gender, religious affiliation, race/ethnicity
**Top ATS Systems:** Workday, Greenhouse, Lever, iCIMS, Taleo, SAP SuccessFactors, Oracle HCM

---

### Canada
**Format:** Resume; CV for academic/research/government
**Length:** 2 pages for most professional roles; 1 page for new graduates
**File Format:** PDF or DOCX
**Language:** Canadian English spelling (colour, honour, labour, organize — note: -ize is acceptable in Canadian English)
**Key Differences from USA:**
- Bilingual capability (English/French) is highly valued and should be noted for federal government and Quebec roles
- Federal government roles via jobs.gc.ca use a competency-based application format with specific screening questions
- Include Canadian provincial licenses/registrations where applicable (e.g., P.Eng. for Professional Engineers, CPA Canada for accountants)

**What to EXCLUDE:** Photo, age, SIN (Social Insurance Number), marital status
**Provincial Notes:** Bilingual CV strongly recommended for Quebec; mention provincial bar admission for lawyers

---

### United Kingdom
**Format:** CV (the term "resume" is not commonly used; UK always says "CV")
**Length:** 2 pages (strictly enforced norm); some senior roles accept 3 pages
**File Format:** PDF or DOCX
**Section Order:**
1. Personal Details (name, phone, email, LinkedIn; home address optional in 2026)
2. Personal Statement / Profile (4–6 lines describing experience, skills, and value proposition)
3. Work Experience (reverse chronological; concise bullet points — UK CVs tend to be less verbose than US resumes)
4. Education (include A-level results; degree class: First, 2:1, 2:2; institution)
5. Skills
6. Interests (optional; include only if genuinely relevant or distinctive)
7. References: state "References available on request" — do NOT list names

**UK-Specific Inclusions:**
- Right to work status if non-UK national (critical post-Brexit; Skilled Worker Visa holders note visa type)
- Professional memberships: CIPD (HR), RICS (Real Estate), ICE/IStructE (Engineering), CFA, ICAEW/ACCA (Finance)
- NMC (Nursing and Midwifery Council) pin number for nurses
- SRA number / bar qualification for solicitors
- For healthcare: GMC registration number for doctors

**What to EXCLUDE:** Generally no photo; no date of birth; no marital status; no nationality (protected under Equality Act 2010)
**Cover Letter:** Expected; concise (1 page max); formal business letter format

---

### Germany
**Format:** Lebenslauf (CV in German)
**Length:** 1–2 pages for the CV itself; full Bewerbungsmappe is longer
**File Format:** PDF only
**Language:** German for most roles; English CV acceptable for international companies, consulting firms, and tech startups in Berlin/Munich

**Section Order:**
1. Persönliche Daten: Name, address, phone, email, DOB, nationality, marital status (optional but accepted)
2. Berufsprofil / Profil (optional 2–3 line summary)
3. Berufserfahrung (Work Experience — reverse chronological with specific dates month/year)
4. Ausbildung (Education — list degrees and vocational qualifications)
5. Kenntnisse (Skills — IT skills, languages with CEFR level, other)
6. Weiterbildungen / Zertifikate (Continuing Education and Certifications)
7. Interessen (optional)
8. Ort, Datum, Unterschrift (Place, date, and handwritten or digital signature)

**Photo:** Professional passport-style Bewerbungsfoto is standard and expected — use a high-quality headshot (white/neutral background, professional attire)
**German Application Package (Bewerbungsmappe):** Full application typically includes:
- Anschreiben (cover letter — addressed specifically to the named hiring manager)
- Lebenslauf (CV)
- Zeugnisse (certificates and diplomas — high school leaving certificate, university degree)
- Arbeitszeugnisse (reference letters from past employers — important; use coded German employer language)
- Lichtbild (photo — can be attached to CV or separate)

**Arbeitszeugnisse Note:** German reference letters use a specific coded language system; "stets zu unserer vollsten Zufriedenheit" (always to our fullest satisfaction) = excellent. Weaker phrasings signal problems.

---

### France
**Format:** CV (Curriculum Vitae)
**Length:** Strictly 1 page (French norm is one page even for senior professionals; maximum 2 for executive roles)
**File Format:** PDF
**Language:** French for all French-language companies; English acceptable for multinational headquarters

**Section Order:**
1. En-tête: Name prominently at top; address, phone, email, LinkedIn
2. Accroche / Profil (optional 3–4 line summary; increasingly used in 2026)
3. Expériences Professionnelles (Work Experience — reverse chronological; concise)
4. Formation (Education — grandes écoles, universities; prestigious schools listed prominently)
5. Compétences (Skills — IT tools, languages, certifications)
6. Langues (Languages with CEFR level: B1, B2, C1, C2, or TOEFL/IELTS scores)
7. Centres d'intérêt (Interests — optional; French employers often read these)

**Photo:** Not legally required but widely accepted; if included, must be professional
**Lettre de Motivation:** A personalized cover letter is critically evaluated; generic letters are immediately dismissed; must explain specifically why this company and this role

**French Cultural Notes:**
- Grandes Écoles (HEC, Sciences Po, École Polytechnique, ENA/INSP, CentraleSupélec) carry tremendous weight in French hiring
- CPGE (classes préparatoires) background noted
- French professional associations: Ordre des Médecins, Barreau, Ordre des Experts-Comptables

---

### Netherlands
**Format:** CV
**Length:** Maximum 2 pages; 1 page preferred for junior roles
**File Format:** PDF
**Language:** Dutch or English depending on company; English widely accepted in Amsterdam, Rotterdam tech and finance sectors

**Dutch-Specific Notes:**
- Dutch employers check LinkedIn extensively before reading CV; optimize your LinkedIn first
- Dutch culture values directness and conciseness — avoid verbose descriptions
- DiSC or MBTI personality type mentioned by some Dutch candidates (cultural norm in some companies)
- Photo: Optional; declining in usage to avoid bias, but still acceptable

**Include:** Dutch language proficiency (NT2 if learned as second language); work permit status for non-EU nationals (essential post-Brexit for UK citizens)
**Cover Letter (Motivatiebrief):** Should be straightforward and concrete; avoid excessive enthusiasm or flattery — Dutch employers find it insincere

---

### Australia
**Format:** Resume
**Length:** 3–4 pages acceptable (Australia allows more detail than USA/UK); quality over conciseness
**File Format:** PDF or DOCX
**Section Order:**
1. Contact Details (name, phone, email, LinkedIn, suburb/city)
2. Professional Summary (3–4 lines tailored to role)
3. Key Skills / Core Competencies (bullet list often precedes work history)
4. Work Experience (reverse chronological; detailed bullet points with outcomes)
5. Education and Qualifications (include professional registrations)
6. Professional Development / Training / Conferences
7. Professional Memberships (Engineers Australia, AHPRA, CPA Australia, CA ANZ, etc.)
8. References (2–3 referees typically listed with name, title, company, phone; OR "Available upon request")

**Australian-Specific Inclusions:**
- Work rights status: Australian citizen, Permanent Resident, or specify visa subclass and work entitlements
- AHPRA (Australian Health Practitioner Regulation Agency) registration number for all regulated health practitioners
- Working with Children Check (WWCC) / Blue Card for education and childcare
- Police Clearance / National Police Check if required by role
- Australian Professional Year for international graduates (note completion)

**What to EXCLUDE:** Age, marital status, religion, race (anti-discrimination laws: Fair Work Act, Equal Opportunity Act)
**Cover Letter:** Expected in most applications; personal, warm, and specific to the role

---

### New Zealand
**Format:** CV or Resume (terms used interchangeably)
**Length:** 3–4 pages similar to Australia
**File Format:** PDF preferred
**NZ-Specific Notes:**
- Reference NZQA qualification equivalency for overseas degrees (NZQA Assessment service at nzqa.govt.nz)
- List NZ professional licensing where applicable: NZRAB (architects), APC (surveyors), practising certificate (lawyers), NZRN registration (nurses via Nursing Council)
- Mention New Zealand residency status or visa type with work rights
- Cover letter is important and should include why you want to live and work in NZ specifically
- NZ employers value cultural fit and personal warmth; the cover letter reflects this

---

### UAE (United Arab Emirates)
**Format:** CV
**Length:** 2–3 pages
**File Format:** PDF
**Language:** English for most corporate roles; Arabic a significant competitive advantage

**Section Order:**
1. Personal Details: Name, nationality, DOB, gender, marital status, current visa status (Employment Visa, Visit Visa, Residence on Spouse's Visa, etc.)
2. Professional Summary
3. Work Experience (detailed with quantified achievements)
4. Education
5. Certifications and Professional Memberships
6. Languages (Arabic proficiency is a competitive differentiator; note IELTS/TOEFL for English)
7. References (optional)

**Photo:** Expected; professional headshot (formal business attire)
**UAE-Specific Requirements:**
- Nationality and visa status are required in UAE applications — not discriminatory in this context
- NOC (No Objection Certificate) may be required to change jobs if currently on an employment visa in UAE
- UAE Golden Visa holders: note visa type as it signals stability to employers
- Dubai vs. Abu Dhabi: Many employers are emirate-specific; note preferred location
- MOHRE (Ministry of Human Resources) and free zone employment: different contract types and protections

---

### Saudi Arabia
**Format:** CV
**Length:** 2–3 pages
**File Format:** PDF
**Language:** Arabic preferred for government and local companies; English for MNCs and Vision 2030 project organizations

**Saudi-Specific Requirements:**
- Iqama (resident permit) status for expatriates — note type and expiry
- Nitaqat (Saudization) compliance: Saudi nationals have quota-based preference in private sector; expatriates note profession aligned with Nitaqat category
- SCFHS (Saudi Commission for Health Specialties) registration for healthcare professionals — mandatory
- Saudi Council of Engineers registration for engineers
- Include date of birth, nationality, gender
- Photo: Expected; professional

**Vision 2030 Note:** Saudi Arabia's Vision 2030 is creating massive demand for talent in tourism, entertainment, tech, construction, and professional services. NEOM, Red Sea Project, Qiddiya, Diriyah are major mega-projects actively recruiting globally.

---

### India
**Format:** Resume or CV (terms used interchangeably; "CV" more common for senior roles)
**Length:** 2–3 pages for experienced professionals; 1–2 for freshers (new graduates)
**File Format:** PDF or DOCX; DOCX still common in India for smaller companies

**Section Order:**
1. Career Objective (freshers) or Professional Summary (experienced)
2. Work Experience
3. Technical Skills (prominently featured for tech roles; include specific technologies)
4. Education (with CGPA/percentage; institution prestige matters greatly — IIT, IIM, NIT, BITS, AIIMS significantly boosts candidacy)
5. Certifications and Courses
6. Projects (critical for freshers; include GitHub URLs, live demo links)
7. Achievements (Hackathons, competitive programming ranks — LeetCode rating, Codeforces, Codechef)
8. Personal Details: DOB, languages known, permanent address, marital status (common in India but evolving)

**Photo:** Common but not required; formal professional photo if included
**Key Distinctions:**
- CGPA/percentage is expected and taken seriously in India hiring; IIT/NIT/IIM pedigree is a strong signal
- For freshers: internship experience at reputable companies (Big 4, FAANG, top Indian startups) is highly valued
- GATE score for engineering; UPSC rank for civil services; CAT percentile for MBA programs

**Job Portals:** Naukri.com, LinkedIn India, Shine.com, Indeed India, Instahyre, Hirist.tech, Internshala (students)
**IT-Specific:** TCS, Infosys, Wipro, HCL hiring processes heavily use their own portals; prepare for online tests (aptitude, coding)

---

### Singapore
**Format:** CV or Resume
**Length:** 2–3 pages
**File Format:** PDF
**Language:** English (official business language of Singapore)

**Section Order:**
1. Personal Particulars: Name, DOB, nationality, NRIC/FIN (for Singaporeans/PRs), employment pass type and expiry (for foreigners)
2. Professional Summary
3. Work Experience (quantified achievements)
4. Education (NUS, NTU, SMU, INSEAD Asia carry strong weight)
5. Skills and Certifications (SkillsFuture certifications are recognized)
6. Languages (English + Mandarin, Malay, or Tamil multilingualism valued)

**Singapore-Specific Notes:**
- MOM (Ministry of Manpower) Fair Consideration Framework: employers must advertise on MyCareersFuture.sg before hiring foreigners
- Employment Pass (EP): S$5,000+/month salary threshold for most professions; higher for financial services
- S Pass: S$3,150+/month; for mid-skilled workers
- Salary expectations sometimes requested upfront in Singapore job listings
- SkillsFuture credits: Singaporeans and PRs can use SkillsFuture credits for approved courses
- Photo: Optional; becoming less common

**Job Portal:** MyCareersFuture.sg (government-run, Fair Consideration Framework compliant), LinkedIn, JobsDB, JobStreet

---

### Japan
**Format:** Rirekisho (履歴書) — standard Japanese resume form
**Length:** Fixed 2-page format (A3 printed or A4 double-sided); Shokumu-Keirekisho (職務経歴書) is an additional skills-narrative document for mid-career applicants
**File Format:** Handwritten (traditional, especially for SMEs and traditional industries); typed PDF increasingly accepted by major companies and startups
**Language:** Japanese; English CVs accepted by international companies and foreign-affiliated firms (gaishi-kei)

**Rirekisho Sections:**
1. Photo: Required — formal headshot (white/blue background, suit)
2. Personal Information: Name (kanji and furigana/katakana), DOB, address, phone, email
3. Education History (学歴): Starting from junior high school; all schools listed chronologically
4. Work History (職歴): All employers listed; include reason for leaving (退職理由)
5. Certificates and Qualifications (免許・資格): All qualifications including driver's license, JLPT, TOEIC
6. Special Skills / Notes (特記事項): Self-introduction, commute time, desired conditions
7. Reasons for Applying (志望動機): Critical section; must be thoughtful and specific
8. Self-PR (自己PR): Brief personal appeal section

**Cultural Notes:**
- Job-hopping (multiple short tenures) viewed negatively; explain transitions clearly
- Employment gaps must be explained
- Loyalty and long-term commitment are valued signals
- Keigo (formal Japanese language) in all written and verbal communication
- JLPT N2 or N1 is typically required for non-Japanese speakers in Japanese work environments
- Shokumu-Keirekisho: Mid-career applicants also submit this free-form document highlighting specific skills, projects, and career achievements (more like a Western resume)

---

### South Africa
**Format:** CV
**Length:** 3–5 pages (South African norm is longer than UK/US)
**File Format:** PDF or DOCX
**Language:** English (primary business language); other official languages noted

**Section Order:**
1. Personal Details: Name, DOB, South African ID number, nationality, gender, ethnicity (B-BBEE relevant), address, phone, email
2. Professional Summary
3. Work Experience (detailed)
4. Education (Matric/NSC through highest degree; SAQA-accredited qualifications)
5. Skills and Computer Literacy
6. Certifications and Professional Memberships
7. References (2–3 professional referees listed with contact details)

**SA-Specific Notes:**
- B-BBEE (Broad-Based Black Economic Empowerment) status is relevant in South Africa and may be included to support employment equity targets
- Valid driver's license and own reliable vehicle often required (public transport gaps)
- Professional registration bodies: HPCSA (health practitioners), SAICA/CIMA/ACCA (accountants), ECSA (engineers), SACAP (architects), SAIBA (bookkeepers)
- Foreign qualifications require SAQA (South African Qualifications Authority) evaluation
- Work permit type for non-South African citizens

---

### Brazil
**Format:** Currículo
**Length:** 1–2 pages (concise is valued in Brazil)
**File Format:** PDF preferred; DOCX also common
**Language:** Portuguese; English for multinationals

**Section Order:**
1. Dados Pessoais: Name, city/state (not full address typically), phone, email, LinkedIn, DOB
2. Objetivo Profissional (Professional Objective — 2–3 lines; specific to each application)
3. Formação Acadêmica (Education — reverse chronological)
4. Experiência Profissional (Work Experience — quantified where possible)
5. Habilidades (Skills — technical and soft skills)
6. Idiomas (Languages with level: básico, intermediário, avançado, fluente, nativo)
7. Cursos e Certificações (Courses and Certifications — Brazilian employers value relevant courses)

**Brazilian-Specific Notes:**
- CLT (Consolidação das Leis do Trabalho) employment is the standard; PJ (Pessoa Jurídica — contractor) increasingly common in tech
- OAB registration for lawyers; CRM for doctors; CRC for accountants; CREA for engineers; CRQ for chemists
- Photo: Optional but common; professional
- CTPS (Carteira de Trabalho) — Brazilian work booklet; now largely digital (CTPS Digital)
- FGTS and INSS: understand social benefits in formal employment

**Job Portals:** LinkedIn Brasil, Catho, InfoJobs, Vagas.com, Gupy (ATS used by major Brazilian companies)

---

### Mexico
**Format:** Currículum Vitae (CV)
**Length:** 2–3 pages
**File Format:** PDF or DOCX
**Language:** Spanish; English for US-linked maquiladoras and MNCs

**Mexico-Specific Notes:**
- RFC (Registro Federal de Contribuyentes — tax ID) and CURP (national ID) used in formal employment paperwork (not in CV typically)
- IMSS (social security) registration expected from formal employers
- Photo: Expected; professional headshot
- Near-shoring boom in 2026: Mexico is a top destination for US companies relocating manufacturing (automotive, aerospace, electronics, textiles); engineering and operations roles in high demand
- Bilingual (Spanish/English) candidates command significant premium especially in border cities (Monterrey, Tijuana, Ciudad Juárez)
- AMPI registration for real estate professionals; Colegio de Ingenieros Civiles / CICM for civil engineers; Barra Mexicana de Abogados for lawyers

**Job Portals:** OCC Mundial, Computrabajo México, Bumeran, LinkedIn México, Indeed México

---
