## 47. GEOPOLITICAL RISK ASSESSMENT FOR CAREER PLANNING — 2026

*Where you work or live carries geopolitical risk. This section helps you assess country stability for long-term career decisions.*

---

### COUNTRY STABILITY INDEXES — KEY SOURCES

| Index | What It Measures | Publisher | Website |
|-------|----------------|---------|---------|
| Fragile States Index (FSI) | 12 stability indicators; 179 countries | Fund for Peace | fragilestatesindex.org |
| Global Peace Index (GPI) | 163 countries; conflict, safety, militarization | IEP | visionofhumanity.org |
| Democracy Index | Political freedom; 167 countries | Economist Intelligence Unit | eiu.com |
| Rule of Law Index | Justice, order, open government | World Justice Project | worldjusticeproject.org |
| Corruption Perceptions Index (CPI) | Perceived corruption 180 countries | Transparency International | transparency.org |
| Human Freedom Index | Personal + economic freedom | Cato + Fraser Institutes | cato.org/human-freedom-index |
| World Governance Indicators | 6 dimensions of governance | World Bank | info.worldbank.org/governance/wgi |

---

### FAILED STATE / HIGH INSTABILITY WARNING COUNTRIES 2026

**Alert Category (FSI Score 90+) — Extreme Caution:**
Yemen, Somalia, Syria, South Sudan, DRC, Central African Republic, Sudan, Nigeria (regions), Myanmar, Afghanistan, Haiti

**Warning Category (FSI Score 70–89) — Significant Risk:**
Pakistan, Zimbabwe, Ethiopia, Mozambique, Mali, Burkina Faso, Niger, Venezuela, Libya, Iraq

**Note:** Always verify current conditions with:
- UK Foreign, Commonwealth & Development Office: gov.uk/foreign-travel-advice
- US State Department Travel Advisories: travel.state.gov
- Australian DFAT: smartraveller.gov.au
- Canada Travel Advisories: travel.gc.ca

---

### CURRENCY COLLAPSE RISK — IMPACT ON CAREER

**Signs of Currency Risk:**
- Inflation >20% per year (hyperinflation risk)
- Large fiscal deficits + weak foreign reserves
- Capital controls (government prevents money leaving)
- Unofficial exchange rate far from official rate

**Recent Collapses and Lessons:**
| Country | Period | Peak Inflation | Impact on Workers |
|---------|-------|---------------|------------------|
| Venezuela | 2016–present | 1,000,000%+ | Professionals fled; doctors became Uber drivers |
| Zimbabwe | 2007–2009 | 89.7 sextillion% | Entire middle class wiped out; emigration wave |
| Lebanon | 2019–present | 220%+ | 75% of population into poverty; skilled exodus |
| Turkey | 2021–2023 | 85% | Real wages halved; tech workers remote for foreign employers |
| Argentina | Ongoing | 140%+ (2023) | Workers demand USD payment; crypto as savings |

**Currency Risk Protection Strategies:**
1. Negotiate salary in USD, EUR, or GBP (possible in remote work)
2. Use EOR services (Remote.com, Deel) if working for foreign employers
3. Keep emergency fund in hard currency account
4. Diversify savings across currencies and countries
5. Consider crypto as inflation hedge (high risk; only small % of savings)

---

### SANCTIONS IMPACT ON EMPLOYMENT

**Countries Under Major Sanctions (Employment Complications):**
| Country | Major Sanctions By | Employment Impact | Work-Around |
|---------|-------------------|------------------|------------|
| Russia | USA/EU/UK (SWIFT exclusion) | Blocked from global banking; talent exodus | Remote for non-sanctioned employers |
| Iran | USA (OFAC comprehensive) | Cannot use USD banking, most western platforms | Limited; regional employment only |
| North Korea | UN + USA + EU | Essentially closed to global economy | N/A |
| Cuba | USA (OFAC) | Limited USD transactions | EU companies can transact |
| Belarus | EU + USA (partial) | Financial restrictions; some tech talent leaving | Remote work for western firms possible |

**OFAC Sanctions List:** home.treasury.gov/policy-issues/office-of-foreign-assets-control-sanctions-programs-and-information

---

### GEOPOLITICAL RISK SCORING FOR YOUR CAREER DECISION

**Use This Checklist Before Relocating for Work:**
- [ ] Country FSI score below 60 (stable zone)
- [ ] No active war or armed conflict in target region
- [ ] Host country not under comprehensive sanctions
- [ ] Local currency inflation under 10%/year
- [ ] Rule of Law Index in top 50% of countries
- [ ] Your home country has diplomatic relations with target country
- [ ] Target country has a bilateral social security agreement with your home country
- [ ] Your profession is in the target country's skills shortage list (protects you from downturns)
- [ ] Research entry/exit restrictions for your nationality (some passports trigger issues)

---

## 48. DISABILITY AND CAREER — GLOBAL RIGHTS, RESOURCES AND EMPLOYERS

*1.3 billion people — 16% of the world's population — have some form of disability (WHO, 2023). This section covers rights, accommodations, disclosure, and inclusive employers.*

---

### WHO DEFINITION AND SCALE

**WHO:** "Disability is part of being human. Almost everyone will temporarily or permanently experience disability at some point in their life." (who.int/health-topics/disability)

**Scale:**
- 1.3 billion people with disabilities globally (WHO 2023)
- 80% live in developing countries
- Employment rate for disabled people 35–40% lower than non-disabled peers globally
- 28% of people with disabilities live in poverty (ILO)

---

### DISABILITY RIGHTS LAWS BY COUNTRY

| Country | Primary Law | Key Protections | Official Source |
|---------|------------|----------------|-----------------|
| USA | ADA (Americans with Disabilities Act, 1990) + ADA Amendments Act 2008 | Reasonable accommodations, equal pay, interview protections, no discrimination | ada.gov; eeoc.gov/disability-discrimination |
| UK | Equality Act 2010 (Disability Chapter) | Reasonable adjustments, protection from indirect discrimination | legislation.gov.uk; equalityhumanrights.com |
| Canada | Accessible Canada Act (2019) + AODA (Ontario 2005) | Federal accessibility standards; provincial employment standards | canada.ca/accessible-canada; ontario.ca/aoda |
| Australia | Disability Discrimination Act 1992 (DDA) | Equal employment, reasonable adjustments | legislation.gov.au; humanrights.gov.au |
| Germany | SGB IX (Social Code Book IX) + BGG (Equal Opportunities for Disabled People) | 5% quota for large employers; sheltered workshops | gesetze-im-internet.de/sgb_9 |
| France | Loi Handicap 2005 | 6% employment quota; AGEFIPH fund for adaptations | agefiph.fr; legifrance.gouv.fr |
| Japan | Act for Promoting Employment of Persons with Disabilities | 2.3% employment quota (April 2024) | jeed.go.jp |
| India | RPWD Act 2016 (Rights of Persons with Disabilities) | 4% reservation in government jobs, accommodation rights | disabilityaffairs.gov.in |
| South Africa | Employment Equity Act No. 55 of 1998 | Affirmative action targets; accommodation requirements | labour.gov.za |
| Brazil | Lei de Cotas (8.213/91) | 2–5% quota for private sector 100+ employees | planalto.gov.br |
| UN (Global) | CRPD (Convention on the Rights of Persons with Disabilities) | International treaty ratified by 185 countries | ohchr.org/en/hrbodies/crpd |

---

### REASONABLE ACCOMMODATIONS — WHAT TO EXPECT AND REQUEST

**Common Accommodations (Legally Protected in Most Countries):**

*Physical/Environmental:*
- Wheelchair accessible workstation and pathways
- Adjustable height desks
- Ergonomic equipment (keyboard, chair, monitor arms)
- Designated accessible parking
- Remote work / hybrid flexibility (major accommodation post-COVID)

*Sensory:*
- Screen reader software (JAWS, NVDA, built-in OS tools)
- Large monitor or text magnification
- Captioning for meetings (Microsoft Teams auto-caption, Otter.ai)
- Sign language interpreter for meetings
- Written instructions instead of verbal

*Cognitive / Mental Health:*
- Flexible schedule for medical appointments
- Quiet workspace or noise-canceling headphones
- Extended deadlines for non-time-critical tasks
- Written rather than verbal instructions
- Regular check-in meetings with manager

*Process:*
- Modified interview format (written vs. spoken, extended time)
- Job coach during onboarding
- Modified training format

**How to Request Accommodations:**
1. You do NOT have to disclose your diagnosis — only that you have a disability requiring accommodation
2. Put requests in writing (email provides record)
3. In USA: covered by ADA Section 504 — employer must engage in "interactive process"
4. If refused unreasonably: file complaint with EEOC (USA), EHRC (UK), CHRC (Canada), AHRC (Australia)

---

### DISCLOSURE DECISION FRAMEWORK

**Should You Disclose?** — Context-Dependent Framework:

| Scenario | Recommend | Reasoning |
|---------|----------|-----------|
| Physical accommodation needed (wheelchair access) | YES — before start date | Essential for logistics |
| Invisible disability; no accommodation needed | Personal choice | No obligation; consider company culture |
| Mental health condition; needs flexible schedule | YES — frame as accommodation need | Protects you legally |
| History of cancer (currently healthy) | Generally NO | Irrelevant to current ability |
| Progressive condition that will worsen | Personal choice + legal protection | Disclosure protects from later "performance" claims |
| Autism/Neurodiversity | Increasingly normalized; company culture dependent | Research company's neurodiversity programs first |

**Pre-Disclosure Research:**
- Google: "[company name] disability inclusion" or "[company name] neurodiversity"
- Check if company signed Disability:IN (disabilityin.org) pledge (USA)
- Check if company has disability ERG (Employee Resource Group)
- Review company's Accessibility Statement on their website

---

### LEADING EMPLOYERS FOR DISABILITY INCLUSION 2026

**USA — Disability:IN Disability Equality Index (DEI) Top Scorers:**
- Microsoft (accessibility.microsoft.com) — Autism Hiring Program; leading accommodation track record
- SAP (sap.com/careers/en/diversity) — Autism at Work program; 1% neurodivergent workforce target
- EY — Neurodiversity Centers of Excellence
- JPMorgan Chase — Autism at Work; Spectrum Scholars program
- Walgreens — Transitional Work Group; distribution center model for disabilities
- Amazon — Disability Leave Services; disability accommodation portal
- IBM — Accessibility Research Center; AT tools development
- Starbucks — Military/veteran + disability hiring programs
- Procter & Gamble — DisAbility Alliance ERG

**UK — Disability Confident Employers (Level 3 Leaders):**
- National Health Service (NHS) — Guaranteed interview scheme
- BT Group — disability confident leader
- Lloyds Banking Group
- Marks & Spencer
Check full list: disabilityconfident.campaign.gov.uk

**Germany:**
- Bundesagentur für Arbeit — publishes quota-compliant employer list
- Rehadat database: rehadat-adressen.de (employers with disability support)

---

| Understood | Neurodiversity careers support | USA | understood.org/careers |

---

### NEURODIVERSITY IN THE WORKPLACE — 2026 LANDSCAPE

**Neurodivergent conditions increasingly recognized in employment:**
- Autism Spectrum Disorder (ASD)
- ADHD (Attention Deficit Hyperactivity Disorder)
- Dyslexia
- Dyspraxia (Developmental Coordination Disorder)
- Tourette Syndrome
- OCD (Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder)
- Dyscalculia

**Skills Often Associated with Neurodivergent Employees:**
- Pattern recognition and anomaly detection (valuable in cybersecurity, QA, finance)
- Deep focus / hyperfocus (software development, research, writing)
- Creative and lateral thinking (design, marketing, innovation)
- Exceptional memory (law, medicine, technical roles)
- Honesty and direct communication (compliance, audit)

**Neurodiversity Programs at Major Companies:**
- Microsoft Neurodiversity Hiring: microsoft.com/en-us/diversity/beyond9to5/cross-disability
- SAP Autism at Work: sap.com/about/company/diversity/autism-at-work.html
- Ford Motor Company Disability & Neurodiversity ERG
- HPE Neurodiversity Program
